рдЗрдкреНрдкрдбрд┐рдпреЗ тАШтАШрддреНрд░реАрдиреН рд▓реЛрдХрд╛рдиреН рд╕рдореНрдкрд░рд┐рдХреНрд░рдореНрдптАЩтАЩ рдОрдйреНрдЧрд┐рд▒рд╡рд┐рдбрддреНрддрд┐рд▓реБрдореН рдХрдгреНрдбреБрдЧреКрд│реНрд╡рджреБред тАШтАШрд╕реНрдирд╛рддреНрд╡рд╛ рднреБрдЮреНрдЬреАрддтАЩтАЩ рдОрдйреНрдЧрд┐рд▒рд╡рд┐рдбрддреНрддрд┐рд▓реН рдХреНрддреНрд╡рд╛рдкреНрд░рддреНрдпрдпрддреНрддрд┐рд▒реНрдХреБ рд╡рд┐рдзрд┐рд░реВрдкрддреНрд╡рдореЗ рдХреКрд│реНрд│рд╡реЗрдгреБрдореН; рдЕрдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрддрддреНрд╡реЗрдирд╛рдиреБрд╡рд╛рджрд╛рд╕рдореНрднрд╡рд╛рддреН ред рдЗрдкреНрдкрдбрд┐рдпреЗ тАШтАШрдкреНрд░рдХреНрд╖рд╛рд▓реНрдпрд╛рдЪрд╛рдореЗрддреНтАЩтАЩ рдОрдйреНрдЧрд┐рд▒рд╡рд┐рдбрддреНрддрд┐рд▓реБрдореН рд▓реНрдпрдкреНрдкреБрдХреНрдХреБ рд╡рд┐рдзрд┐рдкрд░рддреНрд╡рдореЗ рд╕реНрд╡реАрдХрд╛рд░реНрдпрдореН; рдкреНрд░рдХреНрд╖рд╛рд│рдирд╕реНрдп рдкреВрд░реНрд╡рдордкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрддрддреНрд╡рд╛рддреН ред рддрдерд╛ рдЪ рдЗрдЩреНрдЧреБ рддреНрдпрдЬрдзрд╛рддреБрд╡реБрдХреНрдХреБ рдЕрдиреБрд╡рд╛рджрд░реВрдкрддреНрд╡рдВ рд╡рд┐рдзрд┐рд░реВрдкрддреНрд╡рдВ рд╡реЗрддрд┐ рд╡рд┐рд╢рдпреЗ рдХреАрд┤реН тАШтАШрдЕрдХрд┐рдЮреНрдЪрдирдйрд╛рдй рддрдйреНрдйрд┐рд▓реИрдпреИрдХреНрдХрдгреНрдбреБ рдЙрдкрд╛рдпрд╛рдиреНрддрд░рдЩреНрдЧрд│рд┐рд▓реН рдкрд┐рд▒рдиреНрдж рдиреИрд░рд╛рд╢реНрдпрдореНтАЩтАЩ рдОрдйреНрд▒реБ рдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрддрдорд╛рдй рдиреИрд░рд╛рд╢реНрдпрд╛рд░реНрдердХрддреНрд╡рдореН
рд╕реКрд▓реНрд▓реБрдЧреИрдпрд╛рд▓реЗ рддрджреБрддреНрддрд░рдорд╛рдй рд▓реНрдпрдкреНрдкреБрдХреНрдХреБ рдЕрдиреБрд╡рд╛рджрд░реВрдкрддреНрд╡рдореЗ рдХреКрд│реНрд│рд╡реЗрдгреБрдореЖрдйреНрд▒реБ рдПрд▒реНрдкрдбреБрдЧрд┐рд▒рджреБред рддрдерд╛ рдЪ рдЗрдиреНрдж рдЕрдиреБрд╡рд╛рджрддреНрддрд┐рд▒реНрдХреБ рдкреНрд░рдпреЛрдЬрдирдореЖрдйреНрдй рд╡реЖрдйреНрдй рд╡рд░реБрд│рд┐рдЪреНрдЪреЖрдпреНрдЧрд┐рд▒рд╛рд░реН рдЗрд╡реНрд╡рдиреБрд╡рд╛рджрддреНрддрд┐рд▒реНрдХреБ рдЕрдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░ рд╡рд┐рд╢реЗрд╖рддреНрддреИрдХреН рдХрд╛рдЯреНрдЯреБрдЧреИ рдкреНрд░рдпреЛрдЬрдирдорд┐рддрд┐ ред рдЕрдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░рд╡рд┐рд╢реЗрд╖рддреНрддреИ - рдЖрдХрд┐рдЮреНрдЪрдиреНрдпрд░реВрдкрдорд╛рдй рдЕрдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░рд╡рд┐рд╢реЗрд╖рддреНрддреИ,

рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рд╛рд╕-рдкреНрд░рд╕реНрддреБрддрд┐рдГ

рдЕрджрд┐рд▓реН тАШтАШрдкрд░рд┐тАЩтАЩ рдОрдйреНрдЧрд┐рд▒ рдЙрдкрд╕рд░реНрдЧрдореН
рдЕрдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░-рдкреМрд╖реНрдХрд▓реНрдпрддреНрддреИ рд╡рд┐рд╡рдХреНрд╖рд┐рдХреНрдХрд┐рд▒рджреБред

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рдЕрддреНрд░ рдкрд░реАрддреНрдпреН-рдЙрдкрд╕рд░реНрдЧреЗрдгрд╛рдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░-рдкреМрд╖реНрдХрд▓реНрдпрдВ рд╡рд┐рд╡рдХреНрд╖реНрдпрддреЗ ред

English

The preposition pari in parityajya is to indicate the person
who is most competent
or has full competence.

Espa├▒ol

La preposici├│n pari en parityajya es para indicar la persona
Quien es m├бs competente
o tiene plena competencia.

рдореВрд▓рдореН

рдЕрджрд┐рд▓реН тАШтАШрдкрд░рд┐тАЩтАЩ рдОрдйреНрдЧрд┐рд▒ рдЙрдкрд╕рд░реНрдЧрдореН рдЕрдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░рдкреМрд╖реНрдХрд▓реНрдпрддреНрддреИ рд╡рд┐рд╡рдХреНрд╖рд┐рдХреНрдХрд┐рд▒рджреБред

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

резрезтАШтАШрдЕрдирд┐рддреНрдпрдореН рдЕрд╕реБрдЦрдВ рд▓реЛрдХрдореН

“Having reached this world which is perishable and without pleasure, you should resort to me with devotion,”

“Habiendo llegado a este mundo corruptible y sin placer,
deber├нas recurrir a m├н con devoci├│n.”

резрезтАШтАШрдЕрдирд┐рддреНрдпрдорд╕реБрдЦрдВ рд▓реЛрдХрдорд┐рдордВ рдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрдп рднрдЬрд╕реНрд╡ рдорд╛рдореНтАЩтАЩ(рдЧреАрддрд╛ реп-рейрей)

рекреирддрдорд╛рд╣реЛрдмрд┐рд▓-рдпрддрд┐рдГ

рдЕрдиреБрд╡рд╛рджрдкрдХреНрд╖рддреНрддрд┐рд▒реНрдХреБ рдЕрдиреБрдЧреБрдгрдорд╛рдй рджреГрд╖реНрдЯрд╛рдиреНрддрддреНрддреИрдХреН рдХрд╛рдЯреНрдЯрд┐ рджрд╛рд░реНрд╖реНрдЯрд╛рдиреНрддрд┐рдХрддреНрддрд┐рд▓реБрдореН рддрддреНрд╕рдорд╛рдирд╛рд░реНрдердХрддреИрдпреИрдпреБрдкрдкрд╛рджрд┐рдХреНрдХрд┐рд▒рд╛рд░реН рдЕрдирд┐рддреНрдпрдорд╕реБрдЦрдорд┐рддреНрдпрд╛рджрд┐рдпрд╛рд▓реНред

рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рд╛рд╕-рдкреНрд░рд╕реНрддреБрддрд┐рдГ

рдОрдйреНрдЧрд┐рд▒рд╡реН рдЗрдбрддреНрддрд┐рд▓реН “рдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрдп” рдОрдйреНрдЧрд┐рд▒рджреБ рд╡рд┐рдзрд┐рдпреН рдЕрдйреНрд▒рд┐рдХреНрдХреЗ

тАШтАШрдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрдп рд╡рд░реНрддрдорд╛рдирд╕реН рддреНрд╡рдореНтАЩтАЩ

рдОрдйреНрд▒реБ рд╡реНрдпрд╛рдЦреНрдпрд╛рддрдореН рдЖрдйрд╛рд▒реН рдкреЛрд▓реЗ

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рдЗрддреНрдпрддреНрд░ " рдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрдп" рдЗрддреНрдпрд╕реНрдп рд╡рд┐рдзрд┐рддреНрд╡рдВ рд╣рд┐рддреНрд╡рд╛

тАШтАШрдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрдп рд╡рд░реНрддрдорд╛рдирд╕реН рддреНрд╡рдореНтАЩтАЩ

" рдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрдп рд╡рд░реНрддрдорд╛рдирд╕реНрддреНрд╡рдореНтАЭ рдЗрддрд┐ рд╡реНрдпрд╛рдЦреНрдпрд╛рдирд╡рддреН

English

In the (above) sentence:- “having reached” does not state a vidhi or injunction meaning - “Reach this world”.

It only means
‘Being in this world’
or
‘since you are in this world’.

Espa├▒ol

En la oraci├│n (arriba): -
“haber alcanzado” no establece un vidhi o mandato que signifique - “Alcanza este mundo”.

solo significa
‘Estar en este mundo’
o
‘ya que est├бs en este mundo’.

рдореВрд▓рдореН

рдОрдйреНрдЧрд┐рд▒рд╡рд┐рдбрддреНрддрд┐рд▓реН рдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрдп рдОрдйреНрдЧрд┐рд▒рджреБ рд╡рд┐рдзрд┐рдпрдйреНрд▒рд┐рдХреНрдХреЗ

рдЗрдЩреНрдЧреБрдореН

тАШтАШрдкрд░рд┐рддреНрдпрдЬреНрдп рд╕реНрдерд┐рддрд╕реН рддреНрд╡рдореНтАЩтАЩ

рдОрдйреНрд▒реБ рд╡рд┐рд╡рдХреНрд╖рд┐рддрдореН рдЖрдЧрдХреН рдХрдбрд╡рджреБред

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рдЕрддреНрд░рд╛рдкрд┐

“рдкрд░рд┐рддреНрдпрдЬреНрдп рд╕реНрдерд┐рддрд╕реН рддреНрд╡рдореНтАЭ

рдЗрддрд┐ рд╡рд┐рд╡рдХреНрд╖рд┐рддрдВ рдпреБрдХреНрддрдореН ред

English

So also, here,
the words “sarvadharm─Бn parityajya”
do not mean give up all dharmas.
It should be taken to mean:

“You that have given up all dharmas”.

Espa├▒ol

As├н tambi├йn, aqu├н,
las palabras “sarvadharm─Бn parityajya”
No quieren decir renunciar a todo el dharmas.
Debe entenderse en el sentido de significa:

“T├║ que has renunciado a todos los dharmas”.

рдореВрд▓рдореН

тАШтАШрдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрдп рд╡рд░реНрддрдорд╛рдирд╕реНрддреНрд╡рдВтАЩтАЩ рдОрдйреНрд▒реБ рд╡реНрдпрд╛рдЦреНрдпрд╛рддрдорд╛рдйрд╛рд▒реНрдкреЛрд▓реЗ рдЗрдЩреНрдЧреБрдореН тАШтАШрдкрд░рд┐рддреНрдпрдЬреНрдп рд╕реНрдерд┐рддрд╕реНрддреНрд╡рдВтАЩтАЩ рдОрдйреНрд▒реБ рд╡рд┐рд╡рдХреНрд╖рд┐рддрдорд╛рдЧрдХреН рдХрдбрд╡рджреБред

рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рд╛рд╕-рдкреНрд░рд╕реНрддреБрддрд┐рдГ

рдЗрдкреН-рдкрдбрд┐ рдЕрд░реНрдерд╛рдиреНрддрд░рдЩреНрдЧрд│рд┐рд▓реБрдореН рдкреНрд░рдпреЛрдЧрдореН рдЙрдгреНрдбрд╛рдЧреИрдпрд╛рд▓реЗ
рдХреНрддреНрд╡рд╛-рд╢реНрд░реБрддрд┐-рдорд╛рддреНрд░рддреНрддреИрдХреН рдХреКрдгреНрдбреБ
“рддреНрдпрд╛рдЧрдореН рдЕрдЩреНрдЧрдореН” рдОрдйреНрдйрд╡реН рдТрдгреНрдгрд╛рджреБред

English

Since this usage of ‘having done a thing’ (past participle) is met with in other senses also,
it is not right to say that
‘having given up all dharmas’
or ‘giving up all dharmas’
is one of the accessories enjoined for prapatti.

(What is meant is not that
the person should give up
but that, as he is unable to adopt other dharmas,
he should seek the Lord as an up─Бya.)

Espa├▒ol

Dado que este uso de ‘haber hecho una cosa’ (participio pasado) se encuentra tambi├йn en otros sentidos,
no es correcto decir eso
‘habiendo renunciado a todos los dharmas’
o ‘renunciar a todos los dharmas’
es uno de los accesorios ordenado para prapatti.

(Lo que quiere decir no es que
la persona deber├нa rendirse
pero que,
como es incapaz de adoptar otros dharmas,
├йl debe buscar al Se├▒or como un up─Бya.)

If parityajya (having given up) is to be considered (at all) as enjoining what should be done (vidhi),

English

Even this interpretation, which is not the meaning that strikes one immediately
and is therefore a little strained,
is better than the meanings given by Saс╣Еkara and others
that what is intended here
is such as the giving up of the dharmas themselves in their essential nature (svar┼лpa),
because it is not in keeping with any pram─Бс╣Зas
(for in the chapters on prapatti,
it is enjoined that the rites and observances of castes and ─Б┼Ыramas
should (always) be performed).

Espa├▒ol

Incluso esta interpretaci├│n, que no es el significado que salta a uno inmediatamente
y est├б por lo tanto un poco tenso,
es mejor que los significados dados por Saс╣Еkara y otros
eso es lo que se pretende aqu├н
es tal como el abandono de los dharmas mismos en su naturaleza esencial (svar┼лpa),
porque no est├б de acuerdo con ning├║n pram─Бс╣Зas
(porque en los cap├нtulos sobre prapatti,
se ordena que los ritos y observancias de castas y ─Б┼Ыramas
debe (siempre) realizarse).

“рдкреНрд░рдкрддреНрддреНрдпреН-рдЕрд░реНрдердВ рдХрд╢реНрдЪрд┐рджреН рдЕрдкрд┐ рдзрд░реНрдореЛ рдирд╛рдиреБрд╖реНрдареЗрдп” > рдЗрддрд┐ рдкреНрд░рдкрддреНрддреЗрд░реН рдиреИрд░рдкреЗрдХреНрд╖реНрдпрдореН рдЙрдЪреНрдпрдд

English

When we take parityajya as a vidhi or injunction,
it would be appropriate to say that
the meaning of sarva dharm─Бn parityajya is -

“No dharma of any kind need be performed for the sake of prapatti”,

in the sense that prapatti does not require any of them (as aс╣Еgas).

Espa├▒ol

Cuando tomamos “parityajya” como vidhi o mandato,
ser├нa apropiado decir que
el significado de “sarva dharm─Бn parityajya” es -

“No es necesario realizar ning├║n dharma de ning├║n tipo por el bien de prapatti”,

en el sentido de que prapatti no requiere ninguno de ellos (como aс╣Еgas).

Nor can it be held that the option is given to the same person (adhik─Бr─л)
who is capable of performing dharma
either to perform the dharma or to give it up.
This would mean two alternative courses,
one of which is difficult and the other light,
when there is no difference in the object of attainment.

uno de los cuales es dif├нcil y el otro ligero,
cuando no hay diferencia en el objeto de logro.

English

It is true that, in the world, among those that are desirous of wealth,
some choose cultivation of the soil and other such difficult operations,
while others choose lighter professions like dealing in rubies and other gems;
but this option is determined by the differences in capacity or competence among the adhik─Бr─лs.

Espa├▒ol

pero esta opci├│n est├б determinada por las diferencias de capacidad o competencia entre los adhik─Бr─лs.

English

Kooarathalvan’s commentary on the carama ┼Ыloka :-

“You that suffer (from anxiety)
because of the impossibility of adoption of other up─Бyas,
give up everything that has been declared as the means of attaining me
and seek me as (your) refuge (tor salvation)тАЭ–

this commentary, too, means only what has been explained (as the meaning so far)
and is not, therefore, opposed to it.

(In that commentary ‘giving up’ states only what has occurred before (anuv─Бda)
or means only “without doing it as an aс╣Еga required for prapatti.”)

Espa├▒ol

Comentario de Kooarathalvan sobre el carama ┼Ыloka: -

“T├║ que sufres (de ansiedad)
debido a la imposibilidad de adopci├│n de otros up─Бyas,
renunciar a todo lo que ha sido declarado como medio para alcanzarme
y b├║scame como (tu) refugio (para la salvaci├│n)тАЭ–

este comentario tambi├йn significa s├│lo
lo que se ha explicado (como el significado hasta ahora)
y no, por lo tanto, se opone a ello.

(En ese comentario ‘renunciar’ indica s├│lo lo que ha ocurrido antes (anuv─Бda)
o significa s├│lo “sin hacerlo como un aс╣Еga requerido para prapatti”).

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рд╕рдорд╛рд╡рд░реНрддрдирд╛рджрд┐рд╖реБ рдЧреБрд░реБ-рд▓рдШреБ-рд╡рд┐рдХрд▓реНрдкреЛрд╜рдкреНрдпреН рдЕрд╡рд╕реНрдерд╛-рд╡рд┐рд╢реЗрд╖реИрд░реН рдирд┐рдпрдд

рдЗрддреНрдпреН-рдЕрдирднреНрдпреБрдкрдЧрдореЗ

English

It is true that, in such cases, as Sam─Бvartana or the conclusion of the Pr─Бj─Бpatyavrata,
baths accompanied by certain vratas or observances are prescribed
and also (as an alternative) baths without any such vratas (which are easier).
But this option is determined by the condition or the circumstances in which the person is situated.
If we do not take it in this light,
the enjoining of the more difficult alternative would be of no use (for no one would adopt it).

Espa├▒ol

Es cierto que, en casos tales como el Sam─Бvartana o la conclusi├│n del Pr─Бj─Бpatyavrata,
ba├▒os acompa├▒ados de ciertos vratas u observancias son prescritos
y tambi├йn (como alternativa) ba├▒os sin tales vratas (que son m├бs f├бciles).

Pero esta opci├│n est├б determinada por la condici├│n o las circunstancias en las que se encuentra la persona.
Si no lo tomamos desde esta perspectiva,
ordenando la alternativa m├бs dif├нcil ser├нa in├║til (porque nadie la adoptar├нa).

English

There is another (wrong) view that
the adhik─Бr─л competent for prapatti is the person
who has fullness of knowledge or fullness of faith
and that the adhik─Бr─л for up─Бsan─Б is the person
who lacks this fullness of knowledge or fullness of faith.

Espa├▒ol

Hay **otra vista (incorrecta) que
el adhik─Бr─л competente para prapatti es la persona
quien tiene plenitud de conocimiento o plenitud de fe
y que el adhik─Бr─л para up─Бsan─Б es la persona
quien carece de esta plenitud de conocimiento o plenitud de fe.

English

It may be argued that dharmas which are of the nature of refraining (from actions)
and which are understood from prohibitory texts (such as do not kill )
are not activities calculated to protect oneself
and are therefore not opposed to prapatti
and that, owing to this
what is intended here is only the giving up of such activities as are positive (pruvritti)
(and not mere abstentions from activity).

This argument, too, is unsound.

Se puede argumentar que

los dharmas que son de la naturaleza de abstenerse (de acciones)
y que se entienden de textos prohibitorios (como no matar)
no son actividades calculadas para protegerse
y por lo tanto no se oponen a prapatti

y que,

debido a esto
lo que se pretende aqu├н es s├│lo el abandono de aquellas actividades que sean positivas (pruvritti)
(y no meras abstenciones de actividad).

Este argumento tambi├йn es err├│neo.

even abstentions are activities.
Refraining from treasonable activities
is often for the sake of protection of one’s self from the penal code).

this objection would stand
only if the giving up of all dharmas (rites and observances) is enjoined (on the prapanna)
for the rest of his life,

is considered as an aс╣Еga (of prapatti)
to be done only at the time of performing prapatti
and if their resumption is permitted after that performance.

The answer to this argument is as follows:-

If only such activities or dharmas in their svar┼лpa as are likely or possible at the time are enjoined to be given up,

English

Therefore the proper interpretation of the vidhi (if it be taken as vidhi) enjoining the giving up is this:

“Prapatti does not require, as an aс╣Еga or accessory,
any dharma or observance or rite
which is required as an aс╣Еga (such as karma) to up─Бsana (meditation) according to vidy─БsтАЭ.

Espa├▒ol

Por lo tanto, la interpretaci├│n adecuada del vidhi (si se toma como vidhi) que ordena el abandono es la siguiente:

“Prapatti no requiere, como aс╣Еga o accesorio,
cualquier dharma u observancia o rito
lo cual se requiere como un aс╣Еga (como el karma) para up─Бsana (meditaci├│n) seg├║n vidy─БsтАЭ.

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рдЕрд╕реНрдорд┐рдиреН рддреНрдпрд╛рдЧ-рд╡рд┐рдзрд┐-рдкрдХреНрд╖реЗ

рддрддреН-рд╕рддреНрддреНрд╡реЗ рд╜рдкрд┐ рд╡рд┐рд▓рдореНрдмрд╛рдХреНрд╖рдорд╛рдгрд╛рдВ рдЪрд╛рд╕реНрдпрд╛рдВ рдкреНрд░рдкрддреНрддрд╛рд╡реН рдЕрдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░рдГ ред

English

Even in this view
that “parityajya” indicates a vidhi or injunction to give up,
the person competent for prapatti
is one who is incapable of other up─Бyas,
or one who, though capable of other up─Бyas,
is too impatient to endure the delay in attaining the fruit
(which the other up─Бyas might entail).

Espa├▒ol

Incluso en esta vista
que “parityajya” indica un vidhi o orden de rendirse,
la persona competente para prapatti
es alguien que es incapaz de otros up─Бyas,
o alguien que, aunque capaz de otros up─Бyas,
est├б demasiado impaciente para soportar el retraso en alcanzar el fruto
(que los otros up─Бyas podr├нan implicar).

English

If we take this view,
it will not be against any of the pram─Бс╣Зas
(viz. those which enjoin the rites of the varс╣Зas and ─Б┼Ыramas,
and those which enjoin bhakti yoga and the like).

Espa├▒ol

Si tomamos esta vista,
no estar├б en contra de ninguno de los pram─Бс╣Зas.
(a saber, aquellos que ordenan los ritos de los varс╣Зas y ─Б┼Ыramas,

English

Some ─Бc─Бryas, who were conversant with the requirements of a sentence,
thought that the carama ┼Ыloka speaks first (in parityajya) of the person competent for prapatti
(as one who is unable to adopt other up─Бyas)
and then declares by the word тАШekamтАЩ (me alone)
that prapatti as an up─Бya does not require anything else as aс╣Еga or accessory.

Espa├▒ol

Algunos ─Бc─Бryas, que estaban versados en los requisitos de una frase,
pens├й que el carama ┼Ыloka habla primero (en parityajya) de la persona competente para prapatti
(como alguien que es incapaz de adoptar otros up─Бyas)
y luego declara con la palabra ’ekam’ (yo solo)
ese prapatti como up─Бya no requiere nada m├бs como aс╣Еga o accesorio.

English

Others said that the carama ┼Ыloka speaks first of prapatti not requiring anything else as aс╣Еga
and then declares who the competent person is for the easier up─Бya ([enjoined] in the word “vraja”) by the suggestion contained in the word ┼Ыoka or grief (in “m─Б ┼ЫuchaH”)
(for the grief should be the grief
due to the man’s inability to adopt other up─Бyas).

Espa├▒ol

y luego declara qui├йn es la persona competente para el up─Бya m├бs f├бcil (ordenado en la palabra “vraja”)
mediante la sugerencia contenida en la palabra ┼Ыoka o dolor (en “m─Б ┼ЫuchaH”)
(porque el dolor deber├нa ser el dolor
debido a la incapacidad del hombre para adoptar otros up─Бyas).

English

and тАШdeve paribс╣Ыс╕Нatay─Б viditay─БтАЩ (with the knowledge of such qualities of the Lord as His being the Lord of all)
refer only to the kind of knowledge
which enables one to understand
such things as up─Бsanas or the kind of knowledge
which enables a man to have a clear understanding of such things as the qualities of the Saviour,
which is necessary for prapatti.

Espa├▒ol

que permite a uno comprender

que permite a un hombre tener una comprensi├│n clara de cosas tales como las cualidades del Salvador,
que es necesario para prapatti.

“рдЭрдЯрд┐рддрд┐ рдлрд▓-рдкреНрд░рджрд╛рди-рдХреНрд╖рдорд╛ рдкреНрд░рдкрддреНрддрд┐рд░реН рдПрд╡рд╛рд╕реНрдорд╛рдХрдореН рдЙрдЪрд┐рддреЗ"рддрд┐ рдордиреНрд╡рд╛рдиреЛ рд╜рдкрд┐

English

Even when a man has both the knowledge of the other up─Бya (viz. up─Бsana)
and the ability to adopt it,
if he is too impatient to brook delay in the attainment (of the end),
he may be competent for performing prapatti,
if he thinks that only prapatti would secure his object (viz., the quick attainment).

Espa├▒ol

Incluso cuando un hombre tiene tanto el conocimiento del otro up─Бya (a saber, up─Бsana)
y la capacidad de adoptar,
si est├б demasiado impaciente para permitir un retraso en el alcance (del fin),
├йl puede ser competente para realizar prapatti,
si piensa que s├│lo prapatti asegurar├нa su objetivo (es decir, el logro r├бpido).

(the perfect enjoyment of the service of Brahman
which is one’s due on account of one’s essential nature.)

Here also the meaning is

’those who desire to have it quickly’
(i.e. those who cannot brook existence without that enjoyment.)

Espa├▒ol

тАЬEste es el up─Бya para aquellos que desean ─Бnantyam”
(el perfecto disfrute del servicio de Brahman
que es debido a la propia naturaleza esencial.)

Aqu├н tambi├йn el significado es

‘aquellos que desean tener r├бpidamente’
(es decir, aquellos que no pueden soportar la existencia sin ese disfrute).

English

Intensity of bhakti or love means a state of mind
in which the man would cease to exist
if he could not have quick attainment.

Espa├▒ol

La intensidad del bhakti o amor significa un estado mental
en el que el hombre dejar├нa de existir
si ├йl no pudiera tener un logro r├бpido.

English

Though this is not the bhakti yoga enjoined for some adhik─Бr─лs,
yet some get that state of mind
by the grace of Bhagav─Бn due to righteous acts (in previous births).

Espa├▒ol

Aunque este no es el bhakti yoga recomendado para algunos adhik─Бr─лs,
Sin embargo, algunos tienen ese estado mental
por la gracia de Bhagav─Бn debido a actos rectos (en nacimientos anteriores).

English

It is true that, in the case of the prapanna,
the performance of any rite or observance
will prevent the attainment of his end,
because, like the Brahma missile,
it would cease to have any effect,
if any other rite is performed to attain the same end.

Espa├▒ol

Es cierto que, en el caso del prapanna,
la realizaci├│n de cualquier rito u observancia
impedir├б la consecuci├│n de su fin,
porque, como el misil Brahma,
dejar├нa de tener alg├║n efecto,
si se realiza cualquier otro rito para alcanzar el mismo fin.

рднрдЧрд╡рджреН-рднрд╛рдЧрд╡рдд-рд╕рдореГрджреНрдзреНрдпреН-рдЖрджрд┐- рдлрд▓рд╛рдиреНрддрд░реЛрджреНрджреЗрд╢реЗрди рд╡рд╛

English

But if these rites are performed for their own sake
(without the desire for any fruit)
or for such things as the glory of Bhagav─Бn or the welfare of Bh─Бgavatas,
there is no impropriety
(and prapatti would not lose its efficacy).

Espa├▒ol

(sin deseo de ning├║n fruto)
o por cosas tales como la gloria de Bhagav─Бn o el bienestar de los Bh─Бgavatas,
No hay ninguna incorrecci├│n
(y prapatti no perder├нa su eficacia).

English

But it may be asked by some:-

тАЬEven if it is admitted that
the giving up of the dharmas themselves is not enjoined,
it is possible that тАШparityajyaтАЩ ( having given up)
may mean the giving up of (only) the thought
that they are up─Бyas.

Espa├▒ol

Pero algunos pueden preguntar: -

тАЬIncluso si se admite que
el abandono de los dharmas mismos no est├б ordenado,
es posible que тАШparityajyaтАЩ (habi├йndose rendido)
puede significar el abandono de (s├│lo) el pensamiento
que ellos son up─Бyas.

these dharmas in their essential form should be performed as aс╣Еgas or accessories to prapatti,
but without the thought that they are up─Бyas.
If this view were accepted,
then, the view that certain things should be performed after prapatti
merely for their own sake
(without any aim, object or the desire for any fruit)
and as mere service (to the Lord) would become untenable.
(For they would still be aс╣Еgas or accessories
and could not be an end in themselves ).

Espa├▒ol

estos dharmas en su forma esencial deben realizarse como aс╣Еgas o accesorios de prapatti,
pero sin el pensamiento de que son up─Бyas.

entonces, la visi├│n de que ciertas cosas deben realizarse despu├йs de prapatti
simplemente por su propio bien
(sin ning├║n fin, objeto o el deseo de ning├║n fruto)
y como mero servicio (al Se├▒or) se volver├нa insostenible.
(Porque ellos seguir├нan siendo aс╣Еgas o accesorios
y no podr├нan ser un fin en s├н mismos).

English

there would be no essential difference between the bhakta and the prapanna.

(The difference would only be nominal.
The man who has bhakti as the main and independent means
and prapatti as an accessory to it
could be called a bhakta

and the man who adopts prapatti as the main and independent means
and bhakti as an accessory to it
would be called a prapanna,
but both would perform the same dharmas
and there would be no difference in their action.)

Espa├▒ol

no habr├нa diferencia esencial entre el bhakta y el prapanna.

(La diferencia s├│lo ser├нa nominal.

podr├нa llamarse un bhakta

y bhakti como accesorio

pero ambos realizar├нan los mismos dharmas

English

yet as stated in another s┼лtra (3 - 4 - 32),
the karmas ordained for the different ─Б┼Ыramas have to be performed,
as they are enjoined as ordinances or commands;
there is nothing to prevent their performance by the prapanna
since commandments have to be obeyed as such (and for no other reason).

Espa├▒ol

sin embargo, como se indica en otro s┼лtra (3 - 4 - 32),
los karmas ordenados para los diferentes ─Б┼Ыramas tienen que ser realizados,
como est├бn ordenados como ordenanzas o mandatos;
no hay nada que pueda impedir su desempe├▒o por parte del prapanna.
ya que los mandamientos hay que obedecerlos como tales (y por ning├║n otro motivo).

English

Therefore, as neither the performance of these dharmas
nor their giving up is an aс╣Еga to prapatti;
to be without the desire to do what is beyond one’s ability
is a mark of competency (for prapatti).

Espa├▒ol

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рд╢рдХреНрдпрд╛рдирд╛рдВ рдирд┐рддреНрдпрдиреИрдорд┐рддреНрддрд┐рдХрд╛рдирд╛рдореН рдЕрдиреБрд╖реНрдард╛рдирдореН

English

The performance of those duties or rites which are nitya and naimittika
and which are within the range of one’s ability
takes rank as mere service
consisting in the observance of a command.

Espa├▒ol

El desempe├▒o de aquellos deberes o ritos que son nitya y naimittika
y cu├бles est├бn dentro del rango de la propia capacidad
toma rango como mero servicio
consistente en la observancia de un comando.

рди рд╕рдЩреНрдХрд▓реНрдк-рдирд┐рдмрдиреНрдзрдирдореН рее

English

It is only the thought or the will to do what is pleasing to the Lord
that is stated (in the ┼Ъ─Бstras) as an aс╣Еga of prapatti.
The action arising out of that will or thought is not an aс╣Еga.
The rites of the varс╣Зa and ─Б┼Ыrama are the proper thing to do
in virtue of their being the Lord’s command
and not because it is the consequence of the will or the thought
to do what is pleasing to Him.

Espa├▒ol

Es s├│lo el pensamiento o la voluntad de hacer lo que agrada al Se├▒or.
eso se afirma (en los ┼Ъ─Бstras) como un aс╣Еga de prapatti.
La acci├│n que surge de esa voluntad o pensamiento no es un aс╣Еga.
Los ritos del varс╣Зa y ─Б┼Ыrama son lo correcto que se debe hacer
en virtud de que son el mandato del Se├▒or
y no porque sea la consecuencia de la voluntad o del pensamiento
hacer lo que le agrada.

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

English

If so, it may be asked:

“What is the purpose or object of performing those manifold and great acts of service
which cannot be included among the commands to perform nitya and naimittika karma ?”

“┬┐Cu├бl es el prop├│sito u objeto de realizar esos m├║ltiples y grandes actos de servicio
Cu├бl no puede incluirse entre los comandos para realizar nitya y naimittika karma?”

рдореВрд▓рдореН

English

┼Ъr─л Aс╕╖avand─Бr in his Gitarthasaс╣Еgraha says:-

“Among these ekantins
( who are devoted exclusively to the Lord),
the wise man (jnani) is called paramaikanti,
one who has supreme devotion to the Lord
to the exclusion of all other interests.
His being alive is solely dependent on the Lord.
To be united with Him is his only delight;
to part from Him is his (only ) pain.
His mind is always with the Lord.

English

He considers himself as an entity
only because of his meditating on Him,
of visiting holy places (sacred to Him),
and of speaking of Him to others,
of bowing to Him and uttering his sacred names.
His actions are performed with his life-breath, mind, will and the senses all dedicated to Him.

de visitar lugares santos (sagrados para ├Йl),
y de hablar de ├Йl a los dem├бs,
de inclinarse ante ├Йl y pronunciar sus sagrados nombres.

рдЗрдиреНрдж рдЪреЛрджреНрдпрддреНрддреИ рдЗрд░рдгреНрдбреБрд╡рд┐рджрдорд╛рдЧ рдкрд░рд┐рд╣рд░рд┐рдХреНрдХрдХреНрдХреЛрд▓рд┐ рдореБрджрд▓реН рдкрд░рд┐рд╣рд╛рд░рддреНрддреИ рдпрд░реБрд│рд┐рдЪреНрдЪреЖрдпреНрдЧрд┐рд▒рд╛рд░реН рдЗрд╡реНрд╡рд┐рдбрддреНрддрд┐рд▓рд┐рддреНрдпрд╛рджрд┐рдирд╛ ред рд╕рд╛рдХреНрд╖рд╛рджрдкреАрддрд┐, рдЕрдЧреНрд░рдВ рдирдпрддреАрддреНрдпрд╛рджрд┐рд╡реНрдпреБрддреНрдкрддреНрддрд┐рдХрд│рд╛рд▓реЗ рдЕрдЧреНрдиреАрдиреНрджреНрд░рд╛рджрд┐рд╢рдмреНрджрдЩреНрдЧрд│реН рд╕рд╛рдХреНрд╖рд╛рддреНрддрд╛рдЧрд╡реЗ рдЕрджрд╛рд╡рджреБ рджреЗрд╡рддрд╛рдиреНрддрд░рд╡реНрдпрд╡рдзрд╛рдирдордйреНрд▒рд┐рдХреНрдХреЗ рднрдЧрд╡рджреНрд╡рд╛рдЪрдХрдорд╛рдЧреИрдпрд╛рд▓реЗ рд╡рд┐рд░реЛрдзрдорд┐рд▓реНрд▓реИ рдпреЖрдйреНрд▒реБ рд╕реКрд▓реНрд▓реБрдЧрд┐рд▒ рд╕реВрддреНрд░рддреНрддрд┐рдйреНрдмрдбрд┐рдпреЗ, рдирд┐рд░реНрд╡рд╣рд┐рдХреНрдХрд▓рд╛рдорд┐рдбрддреНрддрд┐рд▓реН рдЕрдирдиреНрдпрдерд╛рд╕рд┐рджреНрдзрдЬреАрд╡рд╛рджрд┐рд▓рд┐рдЩреНрдЧрдорд┐рд▓реНрд▓рд╛рджрд╡рд┐рдбрддреНрддрд┐рд▓реН рдОрдйреНрд▒рдмрдбрд┐ред

рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рд╛рд╕-рдкреНрд░рд╕реНрддреБрддрд┐рдГ

рдЕрдЧреНрд░-рдирдпрдирд╛рджрд┐-рд╡реНрдпреБрддреНрдкрддреНрддрд┐-рд╡рд╢рддреНрддрд╛рд▓реЗ
рдЕрдЧреНрдиреНрдпреН-рдЖрджрд┐-рд╢рдмреНрджрдЩреНрдЧрд│реИ рд╕рд░реНрд╡реЗрд╢реНрд╡рд░рдйреБрдХреНрдХреБ рд╕рд╛рдХреНрд╖рд╛рджреН-рд╡рд╛рдЪрдХрдЩреНрдЧрд│реН рдЖрдЧ рдирд┐рд░реНрд╡рд╣рд┐рдХреНрдХрд▓реН рдЖрдореН рдЗрдбрддреНрддрд┐рд▓реН
рдЗрд╡реИ рд╢реНрд░реА-рд╕рд╣рд╕реНрд░-рдирд╛рдорддреНрддрд┐рдйреН рддрд┐рд░реБ-рдирд╛рдордЩреНрдЧрд│рд┐рдйреН рдмрдбрд┐рдпреЗ рдирд┐рд▒реНрдХреИрдпрд╛рд▓реЗ
рдЗрд╡рд▒реНрд▒рд┐рд▓реН рджреЗрд╡рддрд╛рдиреНрддрд░-рд╕реНрдкрд░реНрд╢рдореН рдЗрд▓реНрд▓реИред

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рдЕрдЧреНрд░-рдирдпрдирд╛рджрд┐-рд╡реНрдпреБрддреНрдкрддреНрддрд┐-рд╡рд╢рд╛рджреН
рдЕрдЧреНрдиреНрдпреН-рдЖрджрд┐-рд╢рдмреНрджрд╛рдирд╛рдВ рд╕рд░реНрд╡реЗрд╢реНрд╡рд░рд╕реНрдп рд╕рд╛рдХреНрд╖рд╛рджреН рд╡рд╛рдЪрдХрддреНрд╡реЗрди рдирд┐рд░реНрд╡рд╣рдгреЗ
рдПрд╖рд╛рдВ рд╢реНрд░реАрд╕рд╣рд╕реНрд░-рдирд╛рдорд╕реНрдп рд╢реНрд░реАрдирд╛рдорд╡рджреН рдЕрд╡рд╕реНрдерд╛рдирд╛рджреН
рдПрддреЗрд╖реБ рди рджреЗрд╡рддрд╛рдиреНрддрд░-рд╕реНрдкрд░реНрд╢рдГ ред

English

names like Agni may be considered, on the authority of Jaimini,
as directly referring to Brahman or Bhagav─Бn
for Agni and other such words may be etymologically derived as “agram nayati”.
(He who receives the best part of the offering for Himself) etc.
There is no worship or contact with other deities,
because they are like the sacred names found in Sahasranama (etymologically applicable to Bhagav─Бn).

Espa├▒ol

nombres como Agni pueden considerarse, seg├║n la autoridad de Jaimini,
como refiri├йndose directamente a Brahman o Bhagav─Бn
porque Agni y otras palabras similares pueden etimol├│gicamente derivarse como “agram nayati”.
(El que recibe la mejor parte de la ofrenda para S├н mismo) etc.
No hay adoraci├│n ni contacto con otras deidades,
porque son como los nombres sagrados que se encuentran en Sahasranama (etimol├│gicamente aplicables a Bhagav─Бn).

рдореВрд▓рдореН

рдЕрдЧреНрд░рдирдпрдирд╛рджрд┐рд╡реНрдпреБрддреНрдкрддреНрддрд┐рд╡рд╢рддреНрддрд╛рд▓реЗ рдЕрдЧреНрдиреНрдпрд╛рджрд┐рд╢рдмреНрджрдЩреНрдЧрд│реИ рд╕рд░реНрд╡реЗрд╢реНрд╡рд░рдйреБрдХреНрдХреБ рд╕рд╛рдХреНрд╖рд╛рджреНрд╡рд╛рдЪрдХрдЩреНрдЧрд│рд╛рдЧ рдирд┐рд░реНрд╡рд╣рд┐рдХреНрдХрд▓рд╛рдорд┐рдбрддреНрддрд┐рд▓реН рдЗрд╡реИ рд╢реНрд░реАрд╕рд╣рд╕реНрд░рдирд╛рдорддреНрддрд┐рдйреН рддрд┐рд░реБрдирд╛рдордЩреНрдЧрд│рд┐рдйреНрдмрдбрд┐рдпреЗ рдирд┐рд▒реНрдХреИрдпрд╛рд▓реЗ рдЗрд╡рд▒реНрд▒рд┐рд▓реН рджреЗрд╡рддрд╛рдиреНрддрд░рд╕реНрдкрд░реНрд╢рдорд┐рд▓реНрд▓реИред

рекреирддрдорд╛рд╣реЛрдмрд┐рд▓-рдпрддрд┐рдГ

рд╢рд░реАрд░-рд╢рд░реАрд░рд┐-рднрд╛рд╡рддреЛ рднрдЧрд╡рджреН-рдЖрд░рд╛рдзрдирдореН

рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рд╛рд╕-рдкреНрд░рд╕реНрддреБрддрд┐рдГ

тАШтАШрджреЗрд╡рд╛рдиреН рдЛрд╖реАрдиреН рдкрд┐рддреГрдиреН рднрдЧрд╡рджреН-рдЖрддреНрдордХрд╛рдиреН рдзреНрдпрд╛рддреНрд╡рд╛ рд╕рдиреНрддрд░реНрдкреНрдптАЩтАЩ
(рдирд┐рддреНрдпрдореН)

рдОрдйреНрд▒реБ рдирд┐рддреНрдп-рдкреНрд░рднреГрддрд┐рдЧрд│рд┐рд▓реН рд╢реНрд░реА-рднрд╛рд╖реНрдп-рдХрд╛рд░рд░реН рдЕрд░реБрд│рд┐рдЪреНрдЪреЖрдпреНрдж рдмрдбрд┐рдпреЗ

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

тАШтАШрджреЗрд╡рд╛рдиреН рдЛрд╖реАрдиреН рдкрд┐рддреГрдиреН рднрдЧрд╡рджреН-рдЖрддреНрдордХрд╛рдиреН рдзреНрдпрд╛рддреНрд╡рд╛ рд╕рдиреНрддрд░реНрдкреНрдптАЩтАЩ
(рдирд┐рддреНрдпрдореН)

рдЗрддрд┐ рдирд┐рддреНрдп-рдкреНрд░рднреГрддрд┐рд╖реБ рд╢реНрд░реАрднрд╛рд╖реНрдпрдХрд╛рд░реИрд░реН рдЙрдХреНрдд-рд░реАрддреНрдпрд╛

English

The author of ┼Ъr─л Bh─Бс╣гya has stated in his Nitya:–

“Having pleased the gods, the rishis and the Manes
with oblations and with the thought that they have Bhagav─Бn as their inner self”

etc.

Espa├▒ol

El autor de ┼Ъr─л Bh─Бс╣гya ha declarado en su Nitya:–

“Habiendo complacido a los dioses, los rishis y los Manes
con oblaciones y con el pensamiento de que tienen a Bhagav─Бn como su yo interior”

etc.

рдореВрд▓рдореН

рекреирддрдорд╛рд╣реЛрдмрд┐рд▓-рдпрддрд┐рдГ

English

In Pratardana vidy─Б and the like, we are taught in the ┼Ы─Бstras
that the Supreme Being may be meditated on (or worshipped) in three forms:

  • (one) in His own divine and essential nature,
  • (two), the Supreme Being as having sentient beings as His attribute (or body),
  • and ( three) the Supreme Being as having non-sentient things as His attribute (or body).

Though He is worshipped in these three ways,
the worship is really to the Supreme Being
and not to His attributes (or bodies) (namely the sentient and non-sentient beings).

Espa├▒ol

En Pratardana vidy─Б y similares, nos ense├▒an en los ┼Ы─Бstras
que el Ser Supremo puede ser meditado (o adorado) en tres formas:

  • (uno) en Su propia naturaleza divina y esencial,
  • (dos), el Ser Supremo tiene seres sintientes como Su atributo (o cuerpo),
  • y (tres) el Ser Supremo que tiene cosas no sensibles como Su atributo (o cuerpo).

Aunque ├Йl es adorado de estas tres maneras,
la adoraci├│n es realmente al Ser Supremo
y no a Sus atributos (o cuerpos) (es decir, los seres sintientes y no sintientes).

English

As stated (in these ┼Ыlokas),
it would be a sin for a paramaikantin if other deities are looked upon by him as the Supreme Being,
if they are considered equal (to N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa)
and if he goes to places where other deities are worshipped,
when these deities have nothing to do with his nitya and naimittika rites and observances.

Espa├▒ol

Como indicado (en estos ┼Ыlokas),
ser├нa un pecado para un paramaikantin si otras deidades son consideradas por ├йl como el Ser Supremo,
si son considerados iguales (a N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa)
y si va a lugares donde se adoran otras deidades,
cuando estas deidades no tienen nada que ver con sus ritos y observancias nitya y naimittika.

+++(рдЕрдиреНрдпрдерд╛)+++ рдирд┐рддреНрдп-рдиреИрдорд┐рддреНрддрд┐рдХреЗрд╖реНрд╡реН рдЖрд░рд╛рдзреНрдпрд╕реНрдп

English

Since these deities stand in the position of bodies to the Supreme Being
who is the inner self of all
and who is the object of adoration in these rites and observances (nitya and naimittika),
there is no thought in the mind of the man
(with supreme and exclusive devotion to the Lord)
of these deities being the Supreme Self,
of their being equal to Bhagav─Бn,
of their being independent of the Lord,
of their being objects of adoration
or of their being the dispensers of the fruits of actions.

with the mantras in certain samhit─Бs following the doctrines of the ─Аgamas (P─Б├▒char─Бtra)
which are prescribed specially (to those who follow them).

(S─Бtvatam, Padmam, Jay─Бkhyam, etc. these are the ─Бgama samhit─Бs.)

con los mantras en ciertos samhit─Бs siguiendo las doctrinas de los ─Аgamas (P─Б├▒char─Бtra)
que est├бn prescritos especialmente (a quienes los siguen).

(S─Бtvatam, Padmam, Jay─Бkhyam, etc. estos son los ─Бgama samhit─Бs.)

and that by every one of them there is the attainment of mokс╣гa,
just in the same way as to all the four ─Б┼Ыramas there are Brahma Vidy─Бs (bhakti and prapatti)
and that to every one of them there is the possibility of attaining mokс╣гa.

Espa├▒ol

y que por cada uno de ellos hay el alcance de mokс╣гa,
de la misma manera que para los cuatro ─Б┼Ыramas hay Brahma Vidy─Бs (bhakti y prapatti)
y que para cada uno de ellos existe la posibilidad de alcanzar mokс╣гa.

English

and other such (erroneous) views -

the above (heretical) views which are opposed to the scriptures and the traditional observances (of the good)
supported by right reason or logic
are not to be accepted
by those who desire to stand in sattvam.

respaldado por una raz├│n o l├│gica correcta
no se aceptan
por aquellos que desean estar en sattvam.

English

But no karma or rite which has been ordained as compulsory of performance
should (on any account) be given up.
For it has been stated :-

“The man who does not perform the rites pertaining to the sandhy─Б
is always impure and is unfit for the performance of any (other) rite.
Whatever other rite or karma he may perform,
he will not obtain the fruit thereofтАЭ.

es siempre impuro y es no apto para la realizaci├│n de cualquier (otro) rito.
Cualquier otro rito o karma que realice,
├йl no obtendr├б el fruto de elloтАЭ.

since even such special forms of service (in temples) as the weaving of garlands and the lighting of lamps
cannot be performed without the up─Бdhi (or conditioning factor) of the body, the senses and the like-
even these would have to be given up (by the man who has realised his essential nature (svar┼лpa)).

Their conduct, too, as described in the Itihasas,
was only in accordance with their castes;
if there was any exceptional circumstances (in their lives against the rules of their caste),
it was due to the exceptional instructions or regulations.

(Vidura was cremated according to Brahma Medha rites
because an aerial voice ordered it.)

Espa├▒ol

era s├│lo de acuerdo con sus castas;
si hubo alguna circunstancia excepcional (en sus vidas en contra de las reglas de su casta),
fue debido a instrucciones o regulaciones excepcionales.

(Vidura fue incinerada seg├║n los ritos de Brahma Medha
porque una voz a├йrea lo orden├│.)

y esto se declara mediante el orden contenido en la palabra parityajya (habi├йndose rendido) (en el carama ┼Ыloka).

English
  1. Therefore one should not perform, for the sake of prapatti,
    those things of which one is capable,
    nor should one acquire, for the sake of prapatti, the ability or skill needed to accomplish what one is incapable of.
Espa├▒ol

    aquellas cosas de las que uno es capaz,

necesaria para lograr lo que uno es incapaz de hacer.

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

[[P372]]
рдЕрдиреБрд╡рд╛рджрдкрдХреНрд╖реЗ

рд╕реНрд╡рд╛рд╢рдХреНрддреНрдпрд╛ рддреНрдпрдХреНрддреЗрднреНрдпреЛ рд╡реНрдпрддрд┐рд░рд┐рдХреНрддрд╛рдирд┐
рд╢рдХреНрдпрддреНрд╡рд╛рддреН рдХреНрд░рд┐рдпрдорд╛рдгрд╛рдиреНрдпреН рдЖрдЬреНрдЮрд╛рдиреБрдкрд╛рд▓рдирд╛рджреАрдирд┐

рдЗрддреНрдпреН рдПрддрддреН
“рдПрдХ”-рд╢рдмреНрджреЗ рд╡рд┐рд╡рдХреНрд╖рд┐рддрдВ рднрд╡рд┐рддреБрдореН рдЕрд░реНрд╣рддрд┐ ред

English

If parityajya, on the other hand, is considered as an anuv─Бda or expression of what has already occurred
(namely, the person being incapable of any up─Бya),

then, the word тАШekaтАЩ (me alone) indicates that
among those rites which arise from the Lord’s command
and those which are approved of by him,

there is no connection between such of them
as are performed as being within the range of a man’s ability,
and prapatti.

Espa├▒ol

Si “parityajya” se considera como una anuv─Бda o expresi├│n de lo que ya ocurri├│
(es decir, la persona siendo incapaz de cualquier up─Бya),

entonces, la palabra ’eka’ (yo solo) indica que

entre aquellos ritos que surgen del mandato del Se├▒or
y aquellos que son aprobados por ├йl,

No hay conexi├│n entre ellos
como se realizan como estando dentro del rango de la capacidad de un hombre,
y prapatti.

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рдЕ-рд╡рд┐рд╢рд┐рд╖реНрдЯ-рдлрд▓рддреНрд╡реЗрди

+++(рдкреНрд░рдкрддреНрддрд┐тЖТ)+++ рдмреНрд░рд╣реНрдорд╛рд╕реНрддреНрд░+++(-рдЕрд╡рдорд╛рди)+++-рдиреНрдпрд╛рдп-рд╕реВрдЪрдирдореН рее

English

In the Brahma S┼лtras,
it is declared that
any one of the vidy─Бs (thirty two vidy─Бs or forms of meditation described in the Upaniс╣гads) may be adopted at one’s option,
as all of them yield the same fruit.

By drawing our attention to it,
the injunction for ty─Бga
contained in “parityajya”
may also be taken to suggest that
prapatti is like the Brahma missile,
which proves ineffective if any other up─Бya is also adopted.

Espa├▒ol

En los Brahma Sutras,
se declara que
cualquiera de los vidy─Бs (treinta y dos vidy─Бs o formas de meditaci├│n descritas en los Upaniс╣гads) puede adoptarse a elecci├│n de cada uno,
ya que todos dan el mismo fruto.

Al llamar nuestra atenci├│n a ello,
el mandato para ty─Бga
contenido en “parityajya”
tambi├йn puede ser tomado para sugerir que
prapatti es como el misil Brahma,
lo cual resulta ineficaz
si tambi├йn se adopta cualquier otro up─Бya.

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рд╡рд┐рдХрд▓реНрдкрд┐рддреЗрд╖реВрдкрд╛рдпрд╛рдиреНрддрд░реЗрд╖реБ рдХрд╕реНрдпрдЪрд┐рджреН рдЕрддреНрд░ рдореЗрд▓рдиреЗ
рдмреНрд░рд╣реНрдорд╛рд╕реНрддреНрд░рдиреНрдпрд╛рдпреЗрди рд╡рд┐рд░реЛрдзрдГ рд╕реНрдпрд╛рджреН

рдЗрддрд┐ рдирд┐рд╡рд░реНрддрдирдВ рдЪрд╛рддреНрд░ рд╡рд┐рдзрд┐рдкреНрд░рдХрд╛рд░рд╛рдГ рее

English

3. “If a man were to adopt one of the up─Бyas (other than prapatti)
which are left open to the option (of the aspirant to mukti)”,
it says to him that,
“by the principle of the Brahma missile,
it would conflict with the effectiveness of prapatti.”

(To sum up :-) The forms of injunction may be such as above.

Espa├▒ol

3. “Si un hombre adoptara uno de los up─Бyas (que no sea prapatti)
que quedan abiertos a la opci├│n (del aspirante a mukti)”,
le dice que,
“por el principio del misil Brahma,
entrar├нa en conflicto con la efectividad de prapatti.”

(Para resumir :-) Las formas de orden pueden ser como las anteriores.

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рдЕрддреЛ рд╜рд╢рдХреНрддрд╛рдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░рддреНрд╡рдореН
рдЖрдХрд┐рдЮреНрдЪрдиреНрдп-рдкреБрд░рд╕реН-рдХреНрд░рд┐рдпрд╛ ред
рдЕрдиреН-рдЕрдЩреНрдЧ-рднрд╛рд╡реЛ рдзрд░реНрдорд╛рдгрд╛рдореН
рдЕ-рд╢рдХреНрдпрд╛рд░рдореНрдн-рд╡рд╛рд░рдгрдореН рее

English

Therefore -

(1) incompetence to do those things
that are not within one’s power
gives competence for prapatti; and

(2) (as an anga of prapatti, putting forth) being destitute of all other up─Бyas is a qualification for prapatti;

(3) the dharmas or rites being no accessory or aс╣Еga to prapatti;

(4) the prevention of effort in trying to do what is not possible for one;

(5) the giving up of the desire to do what is beyond one’s ability;

Espa├▒ol

Por lo tanto -

(1) incompetencia para hacer esas cosas
que no est├бn dentro del poder de uno
da competencia para prapatti; y

(2) (como un anga de prapatti, presentando) estar desprovisto de todos los dem├бs up─Бyas;

(3) los dharmas o ritos no son accesorios o aс╣Еga de prapatti;

(4) la prevenci├│n del esfuerzo al intentar hacer lo que no es posible para uno;

(5) renunciar al deseo de hacer lo que est├б m├бs all├б de la propia capacidad;

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рддреНрдпрд╛рдЧреЛрдХреНрддрд┐рд░реН рдЕ-рд╡рд┐рд░реЛрдзрд┐рдиреА ред
рдЙрдкрд╛рд╕рдХреЗ рд╜рдкрд┐ рддреБрд▓реНрдпрддреНрд╡рд╛рджреН
рдЗрд╣ +++(рдкреНрд░рдкрддреНрддрд┐-рдкрд░-рдкреНрд░рдХрд░рдгреЗ)+++ рд╕рд╛ рди рд╡рд┐рд╢реЗрд╖рд┐рдХрд╛ рее

English

The interpretation (which is given by some)
that what is asked to be given up
is the dharmas or rites associated with other deities (than Bhagav─Бn)
is not objectionable,
but as this applies to both the man who adopts bhakti or up─Бsana and the man who adopts prapatti,
this interpretation is inappropriate here
(in the context especially relating to the prapanna ).

Espa├▒ol

La interpretaci├│n (que la dan algunos)
que, lo que se pide se renuncia
son los dharmas o ritos asociados con otras deidades (adem├бs de Bhagav─Бn)
no es objetable,

pero como esto se aplica tanto al hombre que adopta bhakti o up─Бsana como al hombre que adopta prapatti,
esta interpretaci├│n es inapropiada aqu├н
(en el contexto especialmente relacionado con prapanna).

English

“The giving up of up─Бyas”

stated in such passages as the following :-

One should give up the up─Бyas and also the ap─Бyas (those activities that are forbidden )

deber├нa tambi├йn interpretarse de la misma manera.

рдЗрддреНрдпреН-рдЙрдХреНрддрд╡рддрдГ рдкреБрдгреНрдпрд╕реНрдп рдЧреБрдгрд╛рдиреН рд╕рд░реНрд╡рд╛рдиреН рд╡рд░реНрдгрдпреЗрдо рее

English

“Do not endeavour to do what is beyond your power
though you have begun the attempt;
at the outset, it is the part of wisdom to give up the desire to do
what lies beyond your ability;
the path of prapatti does not require any aids ;
if you desire other aids for it,
it will lose its potency like the Brahma missile ;
you are not among those who have the full knowledge
required to follow the path of bhakti or up─Бsana,
which takes a long time to bear fruit;
hence if you seek my feet as your refuge
reflecting on your being destitute of other up─Бyas,
I will pardon all your sins”:

Let us extol the great and good qualities of the holy ┼Ъr─л Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa who spoke these words.

Espa├▒ol

“No te esfuerces en hacer lo que est├б m├бs all├б de tu poder
aunque has comenzado el intento;

lo que hay m├бs all├б de tu capacidad;
